[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2768[0m[39m:          nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest/tls_multirec/patched_mongoose.[0m[1;92mc:2772[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2781[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2772[0m[39m:          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnesting[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2773[0m[39m:          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth == ed && path[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos[0m[1;39m][0m[39m == [0m[32m'[0m[32m[[0m[32m'[0m[39m && ei == ci[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2774[0m[39m:            ed++, pos++, ci = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2775[0m[39m:            for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mei = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; path[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos[0m[1;39m][0m[39m != [0m[32m'[0m[32m][0m[32m'[0m[39m && path[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos[0m[1;39m][0m[39m != [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m; pos++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2776[0m[39m:              ei *= [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2777[0m[39m:              ei += path[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos[0m[1;39m][0m[39m - [0m[32m'0'[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2778[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2779[0m[39m:            if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpath[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mpos[0m[1;39m][0m[39m != [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m pos++;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2780[0m[39m:          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2781[0m[39m:          nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is a **stack-buffer-overflow** caused by a critical mismatch [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbetween:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Buffer allocation**: `unsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` where [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH = [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m30[0m[39m bytes, indices [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m29[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Bounds check**: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` where `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m= [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m`[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Buffer write**: `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = c`[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen parsing JSON with [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m levels of nesting, the check `depth > [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` evaluates to `[0m[1;36m30[0m[39m > [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m` which is FALSE, allowing execution to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue. The subsequent `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` then writes to `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, which is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m byte beyond the allocated [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m-byte buffer.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Locations[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe overflow occurs at **four specific locations** across two files:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **src/json.c**: lines [0m[1;36m167[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m172[0m[39m and lines [0m[1;36m176[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m185[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **mongoose.c**: lines [0m[1;36m2763[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2768[0m[39m and lines [0m[1;36m2772[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2781[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThese locations handle opening braces `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` and opening brackets `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m` when tracking [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJSON nesting depth.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Verified Correct Fix Pattern[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patched reference implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`test/tls_multirec/patched_mongoose.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m shows[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe correct fix:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnesting[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis replaces:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Patch src/json.c[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify **two locations** in the `mg_json_get` function:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m167[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** - when handling `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` character:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- To: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnesting[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;`[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m176[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** - when handling `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m` character:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- To: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnesting[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;`[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Patch mongoose.c[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApply identical fixes to the amalgamated version:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2763[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** - when handling `[0m[1;39m{[0m[39m` character:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- To: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnesting[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;`[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2772[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m** - when handling `[0m[1;39m[[0m[39m` character:[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Change: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- To: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= [0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnesting[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;`[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates the constant mismatch**: By using `[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnesting[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` instead of [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`, the bounds check dynamically reflects the actual buffer size[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m30[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, eliminating the dangerous discrepancy.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Correct timing with `>=`**: The `>=` operator ensures the check occurs BEFORE [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriting to the array. When `depth` reaches [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m, the condition `[0m[1;36m30[0m[39m >= [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m` is TRUE, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreturning `MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP` before `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` can write to the [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds index [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m.[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Type safety**: The cast `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnesting[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` ensures type consistency with [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe `int depth` variable, avoiding compiler warnings.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal invasive change**: The fix modifies only the bounds check logic [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout altering the algorithm, data structures, or API contract.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Matches proven solution**: This approach is identical to the patched reference[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation that already exists in the codebase.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Maintains nesting tracking**: The `nesting` array continues to track opening [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbrackets/braces as designed.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preserves error handling**: The `MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP` error is still returned for[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeeply nested JSON, just at the correct threshold [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m30[0m[39m levels instead of [0m[1;36m60[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Backward compatible**: JSON with ≤[0m[1;36m29[0m[39m levels of nesting will continue to work. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe test case at `test/unit_test.[0m[1;92mc:3161[0m[39m` with [0m[1;36m15[0m[39m levels will still pass.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No API changes**: All [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m dependent JSON functions [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`mg_json_get_tok`, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_json_get_num`, `mg_json_get_bool`, `mg_json_get_str`, `mg_json_get_b64`, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_json_get_hex`, `mg_json_get_long`, `mg_json_next`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m automatically benefit [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout modification.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issue[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Prevents the overflow**: When `depth` reaches [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m, the check triggers BEFORE [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe write, preventing access to `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m30[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Matches AddressSanitizer report**: The crash occurred at line [0m[1;36m185[0m[39m/[0m[1;36m2781[0m[39m when [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwriting the 31st element to a [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m-element array. This fix prevents that write.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Protects read operations**: The `MG_EOO` macro [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m154[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and other code that [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreads `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth - [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` are also protected, as `depth` can no longer exceed the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer size.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigations[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **JSON nesting limit reduced**: The effective limit drops from [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m levels.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is the intended behavior. The buffer was always [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m bytes;[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe check was incorrectly allowing [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m levels. Real-world JSON rarely exceeds [0m[1;36m15[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m20[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlevels of nesting.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Behavior change for [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m+ level JSON**: JSON that previously might have [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincorrectly, with overflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m now returns `MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP`.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is a security fix. The previous behavior was [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mundefined/corrupt; the new behavior is well-defined and safe.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Existing tests**: Any tests expecting [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m+ levels of nesting to succeed will [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfail.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Based on code analysis, the test suite only validates up to [0m[1;36m15[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlevels [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m3161[0m[39m of unit_test.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. No test adjustments should be needed.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe patched reference implementation at `test/tls_multirec/patched_mongoose.c` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m2763[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m2772[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already uses this exact pattern, confirming it's the [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mestablished solution for this vulnerability in this codebase.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy resolves the stack-buffer-overflow by correcting the bounds check[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto use the actual buffer size [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnesting[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m30[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m instead of the incorrect [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconstant [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING = [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The change is surgical, affecting only [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlines across [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m files, and preserves all existing functionality while eliminating [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe vulnerability. The approach is proven by the existing patched reference [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation in the codebase.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
